<script>

    function saveStudentDetailsMoreInfo() {
        
        $.validator.setDefaults({ ignore: ":hidden:not(#CountriesChosen)" })

        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                firstName: $('#FirstName').val(),
                middleName: $('#MiddleName').val(),
                lastName: $('#LastName').val(),
                email: $('#Email').val(),
                mobileNo: $('#MobileNo').val(),
                countriesChosen: $('#CountriesChosen').val(),
                dOB: $('#DOB').val(),
                gender: $('#Gender').val(),
                maritalStatus: $('#MaritalStatus').val(),
                id:789742
            };
            $.post("/StudentApplications/saveStudentDetailsMoreInfo", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    $("#dispName").text($('#FirstName').val() + " " + $('#MiddleName').val() + " " + $('#LastName').val());
                    $("#dispEmail").text($('#Email').val());
                    $("#dispMob").text($('#MobileNo').val());
                    setSuccessAlert('success','Saved');
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetStudentProfileInfo" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#profileMoreInfo').html(resp);
                    });
                }
                else if (resp.errormessage != null && resp.errormessage != "") {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', resp.errormessage);
                }
                else {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }

</script>

<script>
    $(function () {
        $("#MobileNo").intlTelInput({
            initialCountry: "in",
            preferredCountries: ['in', 'bd', 'np', 'lk', 'my', 'vn', 'ng', 'gh'],
            separateDialCode: true,
            nationalMode: false,
            hiddenInput: "full_phone"
        });

        $("#MobileNo").blur(function () {
            if ($(this).val().trim()) {
                if ($(this).intlTelInput("isValidNumber")) {
                    $(this).val($(this).intlTelInput("getNumber").replace(/\s/g, '').trim());
                }
                else {
                    setErrorAlert("Error", "Please enter valid mobile number");
                    $(this).focus();
                }
            }
        });

        if ($("MobileNo").val() != "") {
            $("MobileNo").intlTelInput("setNumber", $("#MobileNo").attr("data-model-value"))
            $("#MobileNo").val($("#MobileNo").attr("data-model-value"));
            $("#MobileNo").focus();
            $("#MobileNo").trigger("blur");
        }

        var previousDOBValue;
        $('#DOB').datetimepicker({
            format: 'L',
            format: 'DD/MM/YYYY',
            useCurrent: false
        });

        // Store the previous value before the picker is shown or changed
        $("#DOB").on("dp.show", function (e) {
            previousDOBValue = $('#DOB').val();
        });


        $("#DOB").on("dp.change", function (e) {
            var currentDOBValue = $('#DOB').val();
            if (previousDOBValue != currentDOBValue && previousDOBValue != undefined) {
                $("#DOB").removeClass('highlight-green');
            }
            var todayDate = new Date();
            var yearToCompare = moment(todayDate, "DD/MM/YYYY").year();
            var yearFromCompare = moment($('#DOB').val(), "DD/MM/YYYY").year();

            if ((yearToCompare - yearFromCompare) < 15) {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'Student should be atleast 15 years old');
                $('#DOB').val('');
                return false;
            }
            else {
                 if (Math.floor(((new Date()) - this.date) / (365.25 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)) < 18) {
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetEmergencyContactInfoForStudent" + "?id=789742&showgc=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#ImportantContacts').html(resp);
                    });
                }
                else {
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetEmergencyContactInfoForStudent" + "?id=789742&showgc=false", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#ImportantContacts').html(resp);
                    });
                }

                $("#DOB").blur();
                
                $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;')
            }

        });

        $("#DOB").on("dp.hide", function (e) {
            $("#DOB").blur()
            
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;')
        });
    });
</script>

<script>
    $('#MailingAddress .selectpicker').selectpicker({
        liveSearch: true
    });

    function saveMailingAddress() {
        
        trimAllFields("#MailingAddress");

        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                addressLine1: $('[name="MailingAddress.AddressLine1"]').val(),
                addressLine2: $('[name="MailingAddress.AddressLine2"]').val(),
                countryId: $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').val(),
                stateId: $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').val(),
                city: $('[name="MailingAddress.City"]').val(),
                pincode: $('[name="MailingAddress.Pincode"]').val()
            };

            $.post("/StudentApplications/SaveMailingAddressData" + "?id=789742", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    setSuccessAlert('success','Saved');

                    if (resp.isPermanentAddressSameAsMailingAddress) {
                        var isEditMode = document.getElementById('PermanentAddress_AddressLine1');
                        var isReadOnly = true;
                        if (isEditMode != null) {
                            isReadOnly = false;
                        }

                        $.get("/StudentApplications/GetPermanentAddress" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=" + isReadOnly, function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#PermanentAddress').html(resp);
                        });
                    }

                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetMailingAddress" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#MailingAddress').html(resp);
                    });
                }
                else {
                    if (resp.error_type == 'passport') {
                        setErrorAlert('Error', resp.errormessage);
                    }
                    else {
                        setErrorAlert('Error', 'error');
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }

    $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').on("change", function (event, IsFromPassportDocumentParse = false) {
        $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').empty();
        var countryId = $(this).val();
        ServiceCall.showLoader();
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '/StudentApplications/GetStateLookupsByCountry',
            datatype: JSON,
            data: { 'countryId': countryId },
            success: function (data) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                var cntrl = $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]');
                $.each(data, function () {
                    $(cntrl).append($("<option></option>").val(this['Value']).html(this['Text']));
                });
                $(cntrl).selectpicker("refresh");
                if (IsFromPassportDocumentParse) {
                    var stateidvalue = $('#HiddenMailingAddressStateIdForPassportOCR').val();
                    if (stateidvalue != '' && stateidvalue != undefined) {
                        $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').val(stateidvalue);
                        $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').selectpicker('refresh');
                    }
                }
                else {
                    $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                }
            },
            error: function (data) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
            }
        });
    });

        
    $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').on("change", function () {
        var mailingAddressStateId = $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').val();
        var passportNumber = $('[name="Passport.PassportNumber"]').val();
        if (passportNumber != "") {
            var isValidated = !ValidateStatePassportNumber(mailingAddressStateId, 0, passportNumber);
            $('[name="Passport.PassportNumber"]').valid();
            if (isValidated) {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please enter a valid passport number');
            }
        }
    });
    


    $(".mailing-address").on("input", function () {
        if ($('#chkIsSameMailing').prop("checked")) {
            var permanentAddressControl = $('[name="' + $(this).attr("name").replace("MailingAddress", "PermanentAddress") + '"]');
            permanentAddressControl.val($(this).val());
            if (permanentAddressControl.is("select")) {
                permanentAddressControl.trigger("change");
            }
        }
    });

    $(".mailing-address select.selectpicker").on("change", function () {
        if ($('#chkIsSameMailing').prop("checked")) {
            var permanentAddressControl = $('[name="' + $(this).attr("name").replace("MailingAddress", "PermanentAddress") + '"]');
            permanentAddressControl.val($(this).val());
            permanentAddressControl.trigger("change");
            permanentAddressControl.selectpicker("refresh")
        }
    });

    $(document).ready(function () {
        updateCheckboxDisabledState();
    });

    $('.mailing-address').on("change", updateCheckboxDisabledState);

    function updateCheckboxDisabledState() {
        var mailingAddressData = {
            addressLine1: $('[name="MailingAddress.AddressLine1"]').val(),
            countryId: $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').val(),
            stateId: $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').val(),
            city: $('[name="MailingAddress.City"]').val(),
            pincode: $('[name="MailingAddress.Pincode"]').val(),
        };
        var sameMailingValue = false;
        for (var mailingaddressDetails in mailingAddressData) {
            if (mailingAddressData.hasOwnProperty(mailingaddressDetails) && (mailingAddressData[mailingaddressDetails] === "" || mailingAddressData[mailingaddressDetails] === null)) {
                sameMailingValue = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        $("#chkIsSameMailing").prop("disabled", sameMailingValue);
        if (sameMailingValue == true) {
            $("#chkIsSameMailing").addClass("MS-tabs Samemaillingaddress samemailing-checkbox");
            $(".mailingaddress-tooltip .bottom").show();
        }
        else {
            $("#chkIsSameMailing").removeClass("MS-tabs Samemaillingaddress samemailing-checkbox");
            $(".mailingaddress-tooltip .bottom").hide();
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    $('#PermanentAddress .selectpicker').selectpicker({
        liveSearch: true
    });

    function savePermanentAddress() {
        
        trimAllFields("#PermanentAddress");

        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                addressLine1: $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine1"]').val(),
                addressLine2: $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine2"]').val(),
                countryId: $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').val(),
                stateId: $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').val(),
                city: $('[name="PermanentAddress.City"]').val(),
                pincode: $('[name="PermanentAddress.Pincode"]').val(),
                SameAsMailingAddress: $('#chkIsSameMailing').prop("checked")
            };

            $.post("/StudentApplications/SavePermanentAddressData" + "?id=789742", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    setSuccessAlert('success','Saved');
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetPermanentAddress" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#PermanentAddress').html(resp);
                    });

                    studentAvanseBanner();
                }
                else {
                    if (resp.error_type == 'passport') {
                        setErrorAlert('Error', resp.errormessage);
                    }
                    else {
                        setErrorAlert('Error', 'error');
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }

    var ischksame = 0;


    $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').on("change", function (event, IsFromPassportDocumentParse = false) {
        var countryId = $(this).val();

        ServiceCall.showLoader();
        $.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: '/StudentApplications/GetStateLookupsByCountry',
            datatype: JSON,
            data: { 'countryId': countryId },
            success: function (data) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                var cntrl = $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]');

                $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').empty();

                $.each(data, function () {
                    $(cntrl).append($("<option></option>").val(this['Value']).html(this['Text']));
                });
                $(cntrl).selectpicker("refresh");
                if (ischksame == 1) {
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').val($('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').val() ?? '');
                    if ($('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').val() == null) {
                        $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').val("");
                    }
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').selectpicker("refresh");
                }
                if (IsFromPassportDocumentParse) {
                    var stateidvalue = $('#HiddenPermanentAddressStateIdForPassportOCR').val();
                    if (stateidvalue != '' && stateidvalue != undefined) {
                        $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').val(stateidvalue);
                        $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').selectpicker("refresh");
                    }
                }
                else {
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                }
            },
            error: function (data) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
             }
            });
    });

    $('#chkIsSameMailing').on('click', function () {
        if ($('#chkIsSameMailing').is(':checked')) {
            ischksame = 1;
            // same as mailing address
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine1"]').val($('[name="MailingAddress.AddressLine1"]').val() ?? '');
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine2"]').val($('[name="MailingAddress.AddressLine2"]').val() ?? '');
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').val($('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').val() ?? '');
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').selectpicker("refresh");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').trigger("change");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.City"]').val($('[name="MailingAddress.City"]').val() ?? '');
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.Pincode"]').val($('[name="MailingAddress.Pincode"]').val() ?? '');

            // remove autoFilled highlights for PermanentAddress when IsSameMailingAddress checked
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine1"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.City"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.Pincode"]').removeClass('highlight-green');

        } else {
            ischksame = 0;
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine1"]').val("");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.AddressLine2"]').val("");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').val("");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').selectpicker("refresh");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').trigger("change");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.City"]').val("");
            $('[name="PermanentAddress.Pincode"]').val("");
        }
    });

    $(".permanent-address").on("blur", function () {
        if ($('#chkIsSameMailing').prop("checked")) {
            if ($(this).val() != ($('[name="' + $(this).attr("name").replace("PermanentAddress", "MailingAddress") + '"]').val() ?? $(this).attr("data-mailingaddress-value"))) {
                $('#chkIsSameMailing').prop("checked", false)
                ischksame = 0;
            }
        }
    });
    $(document).ready(function () {
        updateCheckboxDisabledState();
    });

        
    $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').on("change", function () {
        var permanentAddressStateId = $('[name="PermanentAddress.StateId"]').val();
        var passportNumber = $('[name="Passport.PassportNumber"]').val();
        if (passportNumber != "") {
            var isValidated = !ValidateStatePassportNumber(0, permanentAddressStateId, passportNumber);
            $('[name="Passport.PassportNumber"]').valid();
            if (isValidated) {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please enter a valid passport number');
            }
        }
    });
    

    $('.mailing-address').on("change", updateCheckboxDisabledState);

                function updateCheckboxDisabledState() {
                    var mailingAddressData = {
            addressLine1: $('[name="MailingAddress.AddressLine1"]').val(),
            countryId: $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').val(),
            stateId: $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').val(),
            city: $('[name="MailingAddress.City"]').val(),
            pincode: $('[name="MailingAddress.Pincode"]').val(),
        };
            var sameMailingValue = false;
        for (var mailingaddressDetails in mailingAddressData) {
            if (mailingAddressData.hasOwnProperty(mailingaddressDetails) && (mailingAddressData[mailingaddressDetails] === "" || mailingAddressData[mailingaddressDetails] === null)) {
                sameMailingValue = true;
                break;
            }
    }
        $("#chkIsSameMailing").prop("disabled", sameMailingValue);
    if (sameMailingValue == true) {
            $("#chkIsSameMailing").addClass("MS-tabs Samemaillingaddress samemailing-checkbox");
            $(".mailingaddress-tooltip .bottom").show();
    }
    else {
            $("#chkIsSameMailing").removeClass("MS-tabs Samemaillingaddress samemailing-checkbox");
            $(".mailingaddress-tooltip .bottom").hide();
    }
    }
</script>

    </div>

<script>

    function GetSpecificDate() {
        var date = new Date(), y = date.getFullYear(), m = date.getMonth();
        var firstDay = new Date(y, m, 1);
        var lastDay = new Date(y, m + 1, 0);

        return new Date((new Date().getFullYear()) + 10, m, lastDay.getDay())
    }
</script>

<script>
    $('#PassportInformation .selectpicker').selectpicker({
        liveSearch: true
    });

    function savePassportInfo() {
        
        trimAllFields("#PassportInformation");

        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                passportNumber: $('[name="Passport.PassportNumber"]').val(),
                issueDate: $('[name="Passport.IssueDate"]').val(),
                expiryDate: $('[name="Passport.ExpiryDate"]').val(),
                issueCountryId: $('[name="Passport.IssueCountryId"]').val(),
                cityofBirth: $('[name="Passport.CityofBirth"]').val(),
                countryOfBirthId: $('[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]').val(),
            };
            $.post("/StudentApplications/SavePassportData" + "?id=789742", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    setSuccessAlert('success','Saved');
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetPassportInformation" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#PassportInformation').html(resp);
                    });
                } else if (resp.error_type == "passport") {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', resp.errormessage);
                }
                else {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'error');
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }

</script>


<script>
    $(function () {
        var previousPassportExpiryDateValue;
        var previousPassportIssueDateValue;
        $('#PassportIssueDate').datetimepicker({
            format: 'L',
            format: 'DD/MM/YYYY',
            useCurrent: false
        });

        // Store the previous value before the picker is shown or changed
        $("#PassportIssueDate").on("dp.show", function (e) {
            previousPassportIssueDateValue = $('#DOB').val();
        });

        $("#PassportIssueDate").on("dp.change", function (e) {
            var currentPassportIssueDateValue = $('#PassportExpiryDate').val();

            if (previousPassportIssueDateValue != currentPassportIssueDateValue && previousPassportIssueDateValue != undefined) {
                $("#PassportIssueDate").removeClass('highlight-green');
            }

            var someDateString = moment().format("DD/MM/YYYY");
            var now = moment(someDateString, "DD/MM/YYYY");
            var issue = moment(e.date, "DD/MM/YYYY");

            if (issue.diff(now) >= 0) {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'Passport issue date should not be the future/today date.');
                $("#PassportIssueDate").val('');
                $('[name="Passport.IssueDate"]').focus();
            }
            $('#PassportIssueDate').blur();
            
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;')
        });

        $("#PassportIssueDate").on("dp.hide", function (e) {
            $('#PassportIssueDate').blur();
            
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;')
        });

        $('#PassportExpiryDate').datetimepicker({
            format: 'L',
            format: 'DD/MM/YYYY',
            useCurrent: false
        });

        // Store the previous value before the picker is shown or changed
        $("#PassportExpiryDate").on("dp.show", function (e) {
            previousPassportExpiryDateValue = $('#DOB').val();
        });

        $("#PassportExpiryDate").on("dp.change", function (e) {

            var currentPassportExpiryDateValue = $('#PassportExpiryDate').val();
            if (previousPassportExpiryDateValue != currentPassportExpiryDateValue && previousPassportExpiryDateValue != undefined) {
                $("#PassportExpiryDate").removeClass('highlight-green');
            }

            var someDateString = moment().format("DD/MM/YYYY");
            var now = moment(someDateString, "DD/MM/YYYY");
            var expiry = moment(e.date, "DD/MM/YYYY");

            if (moment.duration(expiry.diff(now, 'days', true), 'days') <= 0) {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'Back dates are not allowed');
                $("#PassportExpiryDate").val('');
                return false;
            }
            now = now.add('months', 6);
            if (!expiry.isAfter(now)) {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'On the date of application the passport expiry should be atleast 6 months valid.');
                $("#PassportExpiryDate").val('');
                $('[name="Passport.ExpiryDate"]').focus();
            }
            $('#PassportExpiryDate').blur();
            
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;')
        });

        $("#PassportExpiryDate").on("dp.hide", function (e) {
            $('#PassportExpiryDate').blur();
            
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;')
        });
    });
</script>

<script>
    $('#Nationality .selectpicker').selectpicker({
        liveSearch: true
    });

    var tsCitizenshipCountry = new TomSelect("#chooseCitizenshipCountry", {
        plugins: ['remove_button'],
        persist: false,
        create: false,
        hidePlaceholder: true,
        closeAfterSelect: true
    });

    $(function () {
        //Nationality Switch Toggle Buttons
        $("input[name='IsMultipleCitizen']").click(function () {
            if ($("#chkYes").is(":checked")) {
                tsCitizenshipCountry.enable();
                $("[name='Nationality.IsMultipleCitizen']").val(true);
            } else {
                $("#chooseCitizenshipCountry").val("");
                tsCitizenshipCountry.sync();
                tsCitizenshipCountry.disable();
                $("[name='Nationality.IsMultipleCitizen']").val(false);
            }
        });

        $("input[name='IsLivingUS']").click(function () {
            if ($("#lusYes").is(":checked")) {
                $("#LivingCountryId").removeAttr("disabled");
                $("#LivingCountryId").focus();
                $("[name='Nationality.IsLivingUS']").val(true);
            } else {
                $("#LivingCountryId").attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $("[name='Nationality.IsLivingUS']").val(false);
            }
            $("#LivingCountryId").selectpicker("refresh");
        });

        let ismultipleCitizen = JSON.parse('false');
        if (ismultipleCitizen) {
            $("#chkYes").attr('checked', true).triggerHandler('click');
        } else {
            $("#chkNo").attr('checked', true).triggerHandler('click');
        }

        let isLivingUs = JSON.parse('false');
        if (isLivingUs) {
            $("#lusYes").attr('checked', true).triggerHandler('click');
        } else {
            $("#lusNo").attr('checked', true).triggerHandler('click');
        }
    });

    function saveNationality() {
        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                nationalityId: $('[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]').val(),
                citizenshipId: $('[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]').val(),
                isMultipleCitizen: $('#chkYes').is(':checked'),
                isLivingUS: $('#lusYes').is(':checked'),
                citizenCountries: $('[name="Nationality.CitizenCountries"]').val(),
                livingCountryId: $('[name="Nationality.LivingCountryId"]').val()
            };
            $.post("/StudentApplications/SaveNationalityData" + "?id=789742", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    setSuccessAlert('success', 'Saved');
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetNationalityInformation" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#Nationality').html(resp);
                    });
                    studentAvanseBanner();
                } else {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'error');
                }
            });
        } else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }

    $('#chooseCitizenshipCountry').on('change', function (evt, params) {
        $("[name='Nationality.CitizenCountries']").val($("#chooseCitizenshipCountry").val());
    });

    $(".switch").find("input[type='hidden']").remove();
</script>

<script>
    $(function () {
        $('#BackgroundInfo .selectpicker').selectpicker({
            liveSearch: true
        });

        const toggleFields = (radioName, enableFieldIds) => {
        const $yesRadio = $(`input[name='${radioName}'][value='false']`);
        const $noRadio = $(`input[name='${radioName}'][value='true']`);

        $yesRadio.on('change', function () {
            enableFieldIds.forEach(id => {
                $(`#${id}`).removeAttr('disabled').focus();
                if (id == "ImmigrationCountryValue" || id == "RefusalCountryValue") {
                    $("#" + id).selectpicker("refresh");
                }
            });
            $(`[name='StudentBackgroundInformations.${radioName}']`).val(true);
        });

        $noRadio.on('change', function () {
            enableFieldIds.forEach(id => {
                $(`#${id}`).attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                if (id == "ImmigrationCountryValue" || id == "RefusalCountryValue") {
                    $("#" + id).selectpicker("refresh");
                }
            });
            $(`[name='StudentBackgroundInformations.${radioName}']`).val(false);
        });
    };

    toggleFields('ImmigrationCountry', ['ImmigrationCountryValue']);
    toggleFields('MedicalCondition', ['MedicalConditionValue']);
    toggleFields('RefusalCountry', ['RefusalCountryValue', 'RefusalCountryAdditional']);
    toggleFields('CriminalOffence', ['CriminalOffenceValue']);

    const initializeRadioState = (radioName, isYes) => {
        const $radio = isYes ? $(`input[name='${radioName}'][value='false']`) : $(`input[name='${radioName}'][value='true']`);
        $radio.prop('checked', true).trigger('change');
    };

    initializeRadioState('ImmigrationCountry', JSON.parse('false'));
    initializeRadioState('MedicalCondition', JSON.parse('false'));
    initializeRadioState('RefusalCountry', JSON.parse('false'));
    initializeRadioState('CriminalOffence', JSON.parse('false'));
});

    function saveBackgroundInfo() {
        
        trimAllFields("#BackgroundInfo");
        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                immigrationCountry: $('#imcYes').is(':checked'),
                medicalCondition: $('#mecYes').is(':checked'),
                refusalCountry: $('#rlcYes').is(':checked'),
                criminalOffence: $('#cloYes').is(':checked'),
                immigrationCountryValue: $('[name="StudentBackgroundInformations.ImmigrationCountryValue"]').val(),
                medicalConditionValue: $('[name="StudentBackgroundInformations.MedicalConditionValue"]').val(),
                refusalCountryValue: $('[name="StudentBackgroundInformations.RefusalCountryValue"]').val(),
                refusalCountryAdditional: $('[name="StudentBackgroundInformations.RefusalCountryAdditional"]').val(),
                criminalOffenceValue: $('[name="StudentBackgroundInformations.CriminalOffenceValue"]').val(),
            };
            $.post("/StudentApplications/SaveBackgroundInfoForStudent" + "?id=789742", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    setSuccessAlert('success','Saved');
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetBackgroundInfoForStudent" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#BackgroundInfo').html(resp);
                    });
                }
                else {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'error');
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            setErrorAlert('Error','Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }
</script>

<script>


    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('#StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber').attr("class", "browser-default");

        var StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber = document.querySelector("#StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber");

        // here, the index maps to the error code returned from getValidationError - see readme
        //var errorMap = ["Invalid number", "Invalid country code", "Too short", "Too long", "Invalid number"];

        // initialise plugin
        var iti1 = window.intlTelInput(StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber, {
            initialCountry: "in",
            preferredCountries: ['in', 'bd', 'np', 'lk', 'my', 'vn', 'ng', 'gh'],
            separateDialCode: true,
            nationalMode: false,
            hiddenInput: "full_phone",
        });

        // on blur: validate
        StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            if (StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber.value.trim()) {
                if (iti1.isValidNumber()) {
                    $("#StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber_I").val(iti1._getFullNumber().replace(/\s/g, '').trim());
                }
                else {
                    setErrorAlert("Error", "Please enter a valid phone number");
                    $("#StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber").focus();
                    return false;
                }
            }
        });

    });
    restrictNonNumericPaste('.phone, #StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber');

    restrictNonNumericKeypress('.phone, #StudentEmergencyContact_ContactNumber');

    function saveMailingAddress() {
        jQuery.validator.addMethod("acceptEmail", function (value, element, param) {
            return value.match(new RegExp("^" + param + "$"));
        }, 'please enter a valid email');
        
        trimAllFields("#ImportantContacts");
        if ($("#formPersonalDetailsAll").valid()) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            var data = {
                contactName: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.ContactName"]').val(),
                contactNumber: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.ContactNumber"]').val(),
                contactEmail: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.ContactEmail"]').val(),
                relation: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.Relation"]').val(),
                guardianName: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.GuardianName"]').val(),
                guardianContact: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.GuardianContact"]').val(),
                guardianAddress: $('[name="StudentEmergencyContact.GuardianAddress"]').val()
            };
            $.post("/StudentApplications/SaveEmergencyContactForStudent" + "?id=789742", data, function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                if (resp.success) {
                    setSuccessAlert('success','Saved');
                    $.get("/StudentApplications/GetEmergencyContactInfoForStudent" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp) {
                        ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                        $('#ImportantContacts').html(resp);
                    });
                }
                else {
                    setErrorAlert('Error', resp.errormessage);
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please fill all required fields');
        }
    }

</script>

    <script>

        $('#personalinformationTab a').on('click', function () {
            var profileStatus = $('#profile').html();
            if (profileStatus == "Complete") {
                $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
            }
        });

        var dropZonePassportOCR = document.getElementById('passportOCR-drop-zone');
        var uploadPassportfileInput = document.getElementById('passportUpload');

        // This is preventing the uploaded file from opening in a new browser window
        function PreventDefaults(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            event.stopPropagation();
        }

        // Prevent default drag behaviors - to handle the events ourselves
        ['dragenter', 'dragover', 'dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(eventName => {
            dropZonePassportOCR.addEventListener(eventName, PreventDefaults, false);
        });

        function HandlePassportOCRDrop(event) {
            var datatransfer = event.dataTransfer; //access the data being transferred
            var files = datatransfer.files; //extract dropped files

            if (files.length > '1') {
                setErrorAlert('Error', 'Only one file can be uploaded. Merge front and back pages of student’s Passport into a single file and try again.');
                return;
            }
            if (files.length == '1') {
                uploadPassportfileInput.files = files;
                uploadPassportfileInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change')); //trigger the change event
            }
        }

        // Handle dropped passport file
        dropZonePassportOCR.addEventListener('drop', HandlePassportOCRDrop, false);


        dropZonePassportOCR.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            dropZonePassportOCR.classList.add('dragover'); // Add highlight class
        });

        dropZonePassportOCR.addEventListener('dragleave', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            dropZonePassportOCR.classList.remove('dragover'); // remove highlight class
        });

        $('#btn-leave').on('click', function () {
            //isleaveConfirmPopupdisplay = false;
            //bindEvent();
            $('body').removeClass('modal-open');
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto;');
            $('#modalSaveBeforeLeave').modal('close');
        });

        $('#btn-save-personal-details').on('click', function () {
            savePersonalDetailsAll()
            isleaveConfirmPopupdisplay = false;
            bindEvent();
            $('body').removeClass('modal-open');
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto;');
            $('#modalSaveBeforeLeave').modal('close');
        });
    </script>
<script>

    function ValidateStatePassportNumber(mailingAdreesStateId, permanentAddressStateId, passportNumber) {
        var isPassportNumberValid = true;

        var passportValidationRequiredStateIdsArray = [1591,1592,1608];

        if (passportValidationRequiredStateIdsArray.includes(parseInt(mailingAdreesStateId)) || passportValidationRequiredStateIdsArray.includes(parseInt(permanentAddressStateId))) {
            var passportNumberRegex = /[A-Z][A-Za-z0-9]{0,8}$/;

            isPassportNumberValid = passportNumber == "" || (passportNumberRegex.test(passportNumber));
        }

        return isPassportNumberValid;
    }

<script src="/bundles/jquery-validate?v=CSfj0NZukiJzVSpSoPEJb0rc1fNkQ1A-PrLJoX8XmgI1"></script>

<script src="/Scripts/moment.js"></script>

<script>
    $(function () {


             $('#btnWorkContinue').click(function () {

                 $('#testSection').siblings().find("a").removeClass('active');
                 $('#testSection a').addClass('active');
                 $('#Tests').siblings().removeClass('active show');
                 $('#Tests').addClass('active show');
                 $('#testSection').trigger('click');
             });

            $('#txtWorkTo').change(function () {

                if ($('#txtWorkFrom').val() != "") {
                                var OstartDate = moment($('#txtWorkFrom').val(), "DD/MM/YYYY");
                                var OendDate = moment($('#txtWorkTo').val(), "DD/MM/YYYY");

                                if (OendDate.isSameOrBefore(OstartDate)) {
                                    setErrorAlert('Error', "End date should be greater than start date");
                                    $('#txtWorkTo').val('');
                                    return false;
                                }
                            }

            });


            $(document).on("click", ".workexperience-details", function () {
                $(this).parent().next().toggle();
            });

            $("#hplnkAddNewWorkInformation").on("click", function (e) {
                $("#divWorkInformationForm").show();
                $("#hplnkAddNewWorkInformationImg").hide();
                $("#hplnkAddNewWorkInformation").hide();
                $('.editbtnWorkExperience').hide();
                $('.removebtnWorkExperience').hide();

            });

        $("#btn-cancel-workexperience").on("click", function (e) {
             ServiceCall.showLoader();
               $.get("/StudentApplications/GetWorkMoreInfo" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp1) {
                            ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                            $('#divWorkExperienceInformation').html(resp1);

                        });

            });


        var workValidator = $("#work-form").validate({
            errorPlacement: function (error, element) {
                $(element)
                    .closest("form")
                    .find(".error")
                    .append(error);
            },
            rules: {
                txtWorkCompanyName: {
                    required: true
                },
                txtWorkDesignation: {
                    required: true
                },
                txtWorkFrom: {
                    required: true
                },
                txtWorkTo: {
                    required: true
                },
                workingradio: {
                    required: true
                }
            },
            messages: {
                txtWorkCompanyName: {
                    required: "Please enter name of the organisation & address."
                },
                txtWorkDesignation: {
                    required: "Please enter position."
                },
                txtWorkFrom: {
                    required: "Please enter working from."
                },
                txtWorkTo: {
                    required: "Please enter working upto."
                },
                workingradio: {
                    required: "Please choose currently working."
                }
          },
          errorPlacement: function (label, element) { // render error placement for each input type
              $('<span class="error"></span>').insertAfter(element).append(label)
              var parent = $(element).parent('.input-with-icon');
              parent.removeClass('success-control').addClass('error-control');
          },

          highlight: function (element) { // hightlight error inputs
              var parent = $(element).parent();
              parent.removeClass('success-control').addClass('error-control');

          },

          unhighlight: function (element) { // revert the change done by hightlight
              var parent = $(element).parent();
              parent.removeClass('error-control').addClass('success-control');
          },
          submitHandler: function () {
              return true;
          },
          invalidHandler: function (event, validator) {
              return false;
          }
      });

        $('#workToggle').change(function () {
            if ($(this).is(':checked')) {
                this.value = 'true';
                $("#txtWorkTo").attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $("#txtWorkTo").val("");
            } else {
                this.value = 'false';
                $("#txtWorkTo").removeAttr("disabled");
                $("#txtWorkTo").focus();
            }
        });

    $("#btn-add-update-work").on("click", function (e) {
      $("#txtWorkCompanyName").val($("#txtWorkCompanyName").val().trim());
      $("#txtWorkDesignation").val($("#txtWorkDesignation").val().trim());
      $("#txtJobProfile").val($("#txtJobProfile").val().trim());

      if ($("#work-form").valid()) {
        if ($('#workToggle').is(':checked') == false) {
          if ($('#txtWorkTo').val() === "") {
            setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please Enter To Date');
            $('[name="WorkExperienceVM.To"]').focus();
            return false;
          }
        }
        if ($('#txtWorkFrom').val() != "") {
          var OstartDate = moment($('#txtWorkFrom').val(), "DD/MM/YYYY");
          var OendDate = moment($('#txtWorkTo').val(), "DD/MM/YYYY");

          if (OendDate.isSameOrBefore(OstartDate)) {
            setErrorAlert('Error', "End date should be greater than start date");
            $('#txtWorkTo').val('');
            return false;
          }
        }

        var formData = {
          workInformationId: $("#WorkInformationId").val() == "" ? 0 : $("#WorkInformationId").val(),
          studentId: '789742',
          companyName: $("#txtWorkCompanyName").val(),
          designation: $("#txtWorkDesignation").val(),
          from: $("#txtWorkFrom").val(),
          to: $("#txtWorkTo").val(),
          iscurrent: $('#workToggle').is(':checked'),
          jobProfile: $("#txtJobProfile").val(),
          modeOfSalary: $("#ddlModeOfSalary").val()
        };

        $.post("/StudentApplications/AddWorkInformation" + "?id=789742", formData, function (resp) {
          ServiceCall.hideLoader();
          if (resp.success && resp.workinfoid != '') {
            setSuccessAlert('success', 'Saved');
            $.get("/StudentApplications/GetWorkMoreInfo" + "?id=789742&isReadOnly=true", function (resp1) {
              ServiceCall.hideLoader();
              $('#divWorkInformationFormNext').html(resp1);
              $("#divWorkInformationForm").hide();
              $("#hplnkAddNewWorkInformationImg").hide();
              $("#hplnkAddNewWorkInformation").hide();
              $('#divWorkInformationForm').find('input:text').val('');
              $('#txtWorkFrom').val("");
              $('#txtWorkTo').val("");
              $('#ddlModeOfSalary').val("");
              $('#btnWorkContinue').hide();
            });
            $('#workExp').removeClass('detail-incomplete');
            $('#workExp').addClass('detail-complete');
            $('#workExp').html('Complete');
          } else {
            setErrorAlert('Error', resp.message);
          }
        });
      } else {
        $("div[class=error]:visible").filter(":first").prev().focus();
      }
    });

        $('input[type=radio][name=workingradio]').change(function () {
            if ($("#workNo").is(":checked")) {
                $("#txtWorkTo").removeAttr("disabled");
                $("#txtWorkTo").focus();
            } else {
                $("#txtWorkTo").attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $("#txtWorkTo").val("");
            }
        });

        });

</script>


<script>
    $(function () {
        $('.working-from').datetimepicker({
            format: 'L',
            format: 'DD/MM/YYYY',
            useCurrent: false
        });
        $('.working-from').on("dp.change", function (e) {
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;');
        });

        $('.working-upto').datetimepicker({
            format: 'L',
            format: 'DD/MM/YYYY',
            useCurrent: false
        });
        $('.working-upto').on("dp.change", function (e) {
            $('body').attr('style', 'overflow:auto !important;');
        });
    });
</script>

        </div>

<script type="text/javascript">

    if ('True' == 'True') {
        //passport OCR logic - start
        document.getElementById("retryAttemptsExceeds").addEventListener("click", function () {
            document.getElementById("passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds").style.display = "none";
        });

        document.getElementById("closeStudentDetailsAutoFilled").addEventListener("click", function () {
            document.getElementById("studentDetailsAutoFilled").style.display = "none";
        });

        document.getElementById("closePassportUploadAttemptsExceeds").addEventListener("click", function () {
            document.getElementById("passportUploadAttemptsExceeds").style.display = "none";
        });

        //show div function - upload passport functionality
        function ShowUploadingPassportDiv() {
            $('#uploadingPassportDiv').show();
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
            $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
            $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
        }

        function ShowStudentDetailsAutoFilledDiv() {
            $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').show();
            $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
            $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
        }

        function ShowAutoUploadFailedDiv() {
            $('#autoUploadFailed').show();
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
            $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
        }

        function ShowRetryAttemptsExceededDiv() {
            $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').show();
            $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
        }

        function ShowUploadPassportDiv() {
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').show();
            $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
            $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
            $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
            $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
        }

        function IsFileSizeValid(file) {
            var maxFileSize = 5242880; // 5MB in bytes
            return file.size <= maxFileSize;
        }

        function IsFileTypeValid(file) {
            var validFileTypes = ['image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/png', 'application/pdf'];
            return validFileTypes.includes(file.type);
        }

        function IsFileNameNotValid(fileName) {
            var ext = fileName.name.lastIndexOf(".");
            var fileNameWithoutExt = fileName.name.substring(0, ext);
            var fileNameFormatRegex = /[`!@#$%^&*()+\=\[\]{};':"\\|,.<>\/?~]/;
            var isNotValid = false;
            if (fileNameFormatRegex.test(fileNameWithoutExt)) {
                isNotValid = true;
            }
            return isNotValid;
        }

        //Highlight for auto filled OCR fields
        function ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled(selector, value) {

            if (selector == '[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]') {
                if (value != 0) {
                    $('[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]').val(value);
                    $('[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]').selectpicker('refresh');
                    $('[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]').addClass('highlight-green');
                }
                else {
                    $('[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                }
            }
            else if (selector == '[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]' || selector == '[Name = "Passport.IssueCountryId"]' || selector == '[name = "Nationality.CitizenshipId"]') {
                if (value != 0) {
                    $('[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]').val(value);
                    $('[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]').selectpicker('refresh');

                    $('[Name = "Passport.IssueCountryId"]').val(value);
                    $('[Name = "Passport.IssueCountryId"]').selectpicker('refresh');

                    $('[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]').val(value);
                    $('[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]').selectpicker('refresh');

                    $('[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]').addClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[Name = "Passport.IssueCountryId"]').addClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]').addClass('highlight-green');
                }
                else {
                    $('[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[Name = "Passport.IssueCountryId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                }
            }
            else if (selector == '[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]') {
                if (value != 0) {
                    $('#HiddenPermanentAddressStateIdForPassportOCR').val(value);
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').val(99).trigger("change", true); // currently api is working for india country and address_country not getting from API in the key format
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').selectpicker('refresh');

                    $('#HiddenMailingAddressStateIdForPassportOCR').val(value);
                    $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').val(99).trigger("change", true); // currently api is working for india country and address_country not getting from API in the key format
                    $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').selectpicker('refresh');

                    $('[name = "PermanentAddress.StateId"]').addClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').addClass('highlight-green');

                    $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').addClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').addClass('highlight-green');

                }
                else {
                    $('[name = "PermanentAddress.StateId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');


                    $('[name="MailingAddress.StateId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');
                    $('[name="MailingAddress.CountryId"]').removeClass('highlight-green');

                }

            }
            else {
                if (value != undefined && value != null) {
                    if (selector != '#DOB' && selector != '#PassportIssueDate' && selector != '#PassportExpiryDate' && selector != '#PermanentAddress_Pincode' && selector != '#Passport_PassportNumber' && selector != '[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]') {
                        value = (value.toLowerCase().replace(/\b(\w)/g, (x) => x.toUpperCase()));
                    }

                    if (selector == '#PermanentAddress_City') {
                        $('#PermanentAddress_City').val(value);
                        $('#MailingAddress_City').val(value);

                        $('#PermanentAddress_City').addClass('highlight-green');
                        $('#MailingAddress_City').addClass('highlight-green');
                    }
                    else if (selector == '#PermanentAddress_Pincode') {
                        $('#PermanentAddress_Pincode').val(value);
                        $('#MailingAddress_Pincode').val(value);

                        $('#PermanentAddress_Pincode').addClass('highlight-green');
                        $('#MailingAddress_Pincode').addClass('highlight-green');
                    }
                    else if (selector == '#Gender') {
                        var genderText = (value == 'F' ? ('Female') : (value == 'M' ? 'Male' : 'Other'));
                        $(selector).val(genderText);
                        $(selector).addClass('highlight-green');
                    }
                    else {
                        $(selector).val(value);
                        $(selector).addClass('highlight-green');
                    }

                }
                else {
                    $(selector).removeClass('highlight-green');
                }
            }

        }

        //Populate field as per the data coming passport OCR
        function PopulateFields(dob, gender, address1, address_pin, address_city, passport_number, stateId, city_of_birth, nationalityCountryId, date_of_issue, expiry_date) {

            //personal information
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#DOB', dob);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#Gender', gender);

            //Mailing address and Permanent Address
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#PermanentAddress_AddressLine1', address1);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#MailingAddress_AddressLine1', address1);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('[name="PermanentAddress.CountryId"]', stateId);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#PermanentAddress_City', address_city);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#PermanentAddress_Pincode', address_pin);

            //Passport Information
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('#Passport_PassportNumber', passport_number);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('[name="Passport.CountryOfBirthId"]', 99);// currently api is working for india country and country_of_birth not getting from API in the key format
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('[Name = "Passport.IssueCountryId"]', 99);// currently api is working for india country and country_of_issue not getting from API in the key format
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('[name="Passport.CityofBirth"]', city_of_birth);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled("#PassportIssueDate", date_of_issue);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled("#PassportExpiryDate", expiry_date);

            //Nationality
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('[name="Nationality.NationalityId"]', nationalityCountryId);
            ApplyHighlightForAutoFilled('[name="Nationality.CitizenshipId"]', 99); // currently api is working for india country and Citizenship not getting from API in the key format
        }
        //Extract value from the parse passport API response
        function GetParsePassportFieldValues(response, keysToRetrieve) {
            var content = response.data.content;
            var orientations = response.data.orientations;
            var collectedValues = {};

            if (orientations) {
                for (var key in orientations) {
                    if (content[key]) {
                        var item = content[key];

                        keysToRetrieve.forEach(keyName => {
                            if (item[keyName] && !collectedValues[keyName]) {
                                collectedValues[keyName] = item[keyName];
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
            return collectedValues;
        }

        function HandleSuccessResponse(response) {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(response.Response);
            var keysToRetrieve = ['dob', 'sex', 'address', 'address_pin', 'address_city', 'passport_number', 'city_of_birth', 'date_of_issue', 'expiry_date'];
            var retrievedValues = GetParsePassportFieldValues(responseData, keysToRetrieve);

            var dob = retrievedValues.dob;
            var gender = retrievedValues.sex;
            var address1 = retrievedValues.address;
            var address_city = retrievedValues.address_city;
            var address_pin = retrievedValues.address_pin;
            var passport_number = retrievedValues.passport_number;
            var city_of_birth = retrievedValues.city_of_birth;
            var date_of_issue = retrievedValues.date_of_issue;
            var expiry_date = retrievedValues.expiry_date;
            var stateId = response.StateId;
            var nationalityCountryId = response.NationalityCountryId;

            PopulateFields(dob, gender, address1, address_pin, address_city, passport_number, stateId, city_of_birth, nationalityCountryId, date_of_issue, expiry_date);
            ShowStudentDetailsAutoFilledDiv();
        }

        function HandleErrorResponse(response, event) {
            if (response.NoOfAttempts == '1' && response.IsFailedFromAPI == true) {
                ShowAutoUploadFailedDiv();
            }
            else if (response.NoOfAttempts >= '2' && response.IsFailedFromAPI == true) {
                ShowRetryAttemptsExceededDiv();
            }
            else {
                ShowUploadPassportDiv();
            }

            setErrorAlert('Error', response.Message);
            return false;
        }

        //Call to parse passport
        function ParseUploadedPassportFile(formData, studentId, event) {
            $.ajax({
                url: '/StudentApplications/NumberOfUploadedPassportHistoryRecords',
                type: 'POST',
                data: { studentId: "789742" },
                success: function (response) {
                    if (response.Success) {
                        var numberOfRecords = response.NumberOfRecords;
                        if (numberOfRecords < '2') {
                            $.ajax({
                                url: '/StudentApplications/ParsePassportDocument?studentId=' + studentId,
                                type: 'POST',
                                data: formData,
                                contentType: false,
                                processData: false,
                                success: function (response) {
                                    if (response.Success) {
                                        HandleSuccessResponse(response);
                                    } else {
                                        HandleErrorResponse(response, event);
                                    }
                                    event.target.value = ''; // Reset the file input after processing
                                },
                                error: function () {
                                    ShowUploadPassportDiv();
                                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'Ooops! Some error occured!');
                                    return false;
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        setErrorAlert('Error', response.Message);
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                    console.error("An error occurred: " + error);
                    return false;
                }
            });

        }

        function HandlePassportUpload(event) {
            ShowUploadingPassportDiv();
            var uploadedPassportFile = event.target.files[0];

            if (uploadedPassportFile) {
                if (!IsFileTypeValid(uploadedPassportFile)) {
                    event.target.value = ''; // Clears the file input
                    ShowUploadPassportDiv();
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'Invalid file type. Please upload a file in JPG, PNG, or PDF format.');
                    return false;
                }

                if (IsFileNameNotValid(uploadedPassportFile)) {
                    event.target.value = ''; // Clears the file input
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'File name must not contain special characters except underscore, hyphen and space. Please rename and upload again.');
                    return false;
                }

                if (IsFileSizeValid(uploadedPassportFile)) {
                    var formData = new FormData();
                    formData.append('passportUpload', uploadedPassportFile);
                    var studentId = "789742";
                    ParseUploadedPassportFile(formData, studentId, event);
                    $('#uploadPassportModal .close').trigger('click');
                } else {
                    event.target.value = ''; // Clears the file input
                    ShowUploadPassportDiv();
                    setErrorAlert('Error', 'Please select a file up to 5 MB.');
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('passportUpload').addEventListener('change', function (event) {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            HandlePassportUpload(event);
            ServiceCall.hideLoader();
        });

        //passport OCR logic - end
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        var personalDetailSection = 'Incomplete';
        if (personalDetailSection == "Complete") {
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();

        }
        else {
            $('#uploadPassportDiv').show();
        }

        // Select the PersonalInformation container
        const personalInfoContainer = $('#PersonalInformation');

        // Function to remove the 'highlight-green' class
        function removeHighlight(event) {
            $(event.target).removeClass('highlight-green');
        }
        // Add event listeners for keyup on input and select elements within the container
        personalInfoContainer.on('input change', 'input.form-control,input, select.form-control', removeHighlight);

        if ('True' == 'True') {
            var personalDetailSection = "Incomplete";

            if (personalDetailSection === "Complete") {
                $('#uploadBtn').addClass('disabled').prop('disabled', true);
                $('#reUploadBtn').addClass('disabled').prop('disabled', true);
                $('#retryAttemptsExceeds').addClass('disabled').prop('disabled', true);
            } else {
                $('#uploadBtn').removeClass('disabled').prop('disabled', false);
                $('#reUploadBtn').removeClass('disabled').prop('disabled', false);
                $('#retryAttemptsExceeds').removeClass('disabled').prop('disabled', false);
            }

            $.ajax({
                url: '/StudentApplications/NumberOfUploadedPassportHistoryRecords',
                type: 'POST',
                data: { studentId: "789742" },
                success: function (response) {
                    if (response.Success) {
                        var numberOfRecords = response.NumberOfRecords;
                        var isFailedResponse = false;
                        if (response.APIResponse != "") {
                            var responseData = JSON.parse(response.APIResponse);

                            if (responseData["error"] != null) {
                                isFailedResponse = true;
                            }
                        }
                        if (personalDetailSection != "Complete") {
                            if (numberOfRecords == 0 && isFailedResponse == false) {
                                $('#uploadPassportDiv').show();
                                $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
                                $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
                                $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
                                $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
                                $('#passportUploadAttemptsExceeds').hide();
                            }
                            else if (numberOfRecords == '1' && isFailedResponse == true) {
                                $('#autoUploadFailed').show();
                                $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
                                $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
                                $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
                                $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
                                $('#passportUploadAttemptsExceeds').hide();

                            }
                            else if (numberOfRecords == '1' && isFailedResponse == false) {
                                $('#uploadPassportDiv').show();
                                $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
                                $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
                                $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
                                $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
                                $('#passportUploadAttemptsExceeds').hide();
                            }
                            else if (numberOfRecords >= '2') {
                                $('#passportUploadAttemptsExceeds').show();
                                $('#passportUploadRetryAttemptsExceeds').hide();
                                $('#autoUploadFailed').hide();
                                $('#uploadPassportDiv').hide();
                                $('#uploadingPassportDiv').hide();
                                $('#studentDetailsAutoFilled').hide();
                            }

                        }

                    }
                    else {
                        setErrorAlert('Error', response.Message);
                        return false;
                    }
                },
                error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                    console.error("An error occurred: " + error);
                }
            });
        }


        $('#QualificationSection').on('click', function () {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            $.get("/StudentApplications/AcademicQualification" + "?id=789742", function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                $('#divQualifications').html(resp);
            });
        });

        $('#testSection').on('click', function () {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            $.get("/StudentApplications/GetTestsData" + "?id=789742", function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                $('#tests').html(resp);
            });
        });

        $('#testEdit').on('click', function () {
            ServiceCall.showLoader();
            $.get("/StudentApplications/GetTestsData" + "?id=789742&isEdit=true", function (resp) {
                ServiceCall.hideLoader();
                $('#tests').html(resp);
            });
        });

    });
</script>
